# M10 Units #17–18 — ʿāwōn family (shared-term family file)

- **File:** wa-m10-units-17-18-avon-family-v1-20260623.md · **v1 · 2026-06-23 · Author:** Claude Code.
- **Units (source: core):** #17 Guilt as inner-being state · #18 Iniquity as accumulated moral crime.
- **Shared term:** a.von H5771 — **one lemma carrying the tri-fold**, split by sub-entry: H5771G "iniquity: crime" (the act / standing wrong) · H5771H "iniquity: guilt" (the incurred liability) · H5771I "iniquity: punishment" (the penalty borne). Plus the guilt-liability band a.sham (H0816), a.shem (H0818), ash.mah (H0819) and the conscience-stagger pu.qah (H6330). 253 verses across the §B substrate.
- **What this file is:** the self-contained evidence home for the two ʿāwōn units — **(A)** general observations (whole ʿāwōn field, flagged) + the two unit sub-sections (collated from the source digests `wa-m10-core-avon-evidence-digest` (AV), `wa-m10-ring2-guilt-evidence-digest` (R2g), `wa-m10-ring1-evidence-digest` (R1) — bonds, threads, held-open items — *nothing of note left behind*), **(B)** the per-verse structured substrate (once; shared across the two units). Flag markers per the index method. Evidence only; **highlight, do not resolve.**
- **Index:** `wa-m10-unit-index-1to32-v1-20260623.md`. **Sources migrated → this unit file** (AV in full; R2g guilt-band; R1 pu.qah row): retained as provenance, superseded as evidence homes for #17/#18.

---

## A. General observations (whole ʿāwōn field)

**Mechanical signature (a.von, 207 occ / 207 verses; from AV §1):** type **status 207/207** (never `action` — a.von is uniformly a standing condition) · faculty **none 207/207** (term-intrinsic; a standing wrong/liability/penalty, not a faculty — interior reads from co-terms only) · valence **sinful 204 / neutral 3** (Num 18:1; 18:23 priestly-charge; 1Sa 28:10 "no punishment"). Sense (the defining diversity): iniquity 115 + iniquities 39 (=154) · **guilt 28** · **punishment 16** · sin 3 · fault 2 · crime 1 · guilty 1 · chastisement 1. Object_type none 99 · abstract 73 · person 26 · God 4 · situation 4. Compound web: partner 382 · qualifier 47 · **co-seated 18** (ne.phesh 9, lev 5, le.vav 2, she.er 1, ba.sar 1). Book spread: Eze 33 · Psa 29 · Isa 24 · Jer 23 · Lev 16 · Job 15 (prophetic + penitential + cultic). **Guilt-liability band (R2g):** a.sham 40 + ash.mah 17 + a.shem 3 = 60 occ, all read. **pu.qah (R1):** 1 occ (the conscience-stagger).

- **⚑ SYNTH — the a.von TRI-FOLD (Thread 2, the defining feature; AV §2a–c, §5).** The same lemma a.von, split only by sub-entry letter, names three things: **CRIME / act-classification (H5771G)** — the wrong itself, often unbounded and accruing ("the iniquity of the Amorites is not yet complete" Gen 15:16; "iniquities of his youth" Job 13:26; "brought forth in iniquity" Psa 51:5); **GUILT / liability (H5771H, 28 occ)** — the standing being-answerable-for, forensic/self-protestation ("God has found out the guilt of your servants" Gen 44:16; "if there is guilt in me, kill me" 1Sa 20:8; "On me alone be the guilt" 1Sa 25:24; 2Sa 14:9); **PUNISHMENT / penalty-borne (H5771I, 16 occ)** — the consequence ("My punishment is greater than I can bear" Gen 4:13; "swept away in the punishment of the city" Gen 19:15; the Ezekiel sign-act "bear their punishment" Eze 4:4,5,6). **One word carrying act + liability + consequence — recorded as diversity, not resolved.** The §10 question: is a.von ONE status carried through act→liability→penalty, or **three different objects** sharing a lemma? The sub-entry split asserts three; the uniform `type=status` + `lemma_meaning=crime` blur them.
- **⚑ SYNTH — the punishment element (H5771I) has no home unit and edges to the external pole (Thread 2; AV §4, §5).** The punishment sense (Gen 4:13; Eze 4:4–6; Job 19:29) describes a *penalty borne*, not an inner-being state — it sits at the seam between inner-being and the **external retribution pole**, and is not the primary home of either #17 (guilt-state) or #18 (accumulated crime). Whether H5771I belongs in M10 (inner-being) at all, or routes to the external pole / a consequence unit, is held open. **Surface for the external-pole synthesis.** (Decomposition: crime = classification, not the act itself; guilt = the inner-being phenomenon; punishment = EXTERNAL retribution — a COLLECTIVE/PROCESS term spanning all three.)
- **⚑ SYNTH — a.von behaves as an object that is borne / visited / blotted-out / remembered (AV §2d).** Five sub-registers, all touching other units: **borne** ("bear iniquity," the priest/scapegoat/Servant — Exo 28:38; Lev 10:17; 16:22; Isa 53:6,11); **visited / generational** ("visiting the iniquity of the fathers" Exo 20:5 = 34:7 = Num 14:18 = Deu 5:9; "we bear their iniquities" Lam 5:7 → feeds #15); **blotted-out / atoned / cast-into-the-sea** (Psa 51:9; 103:3; Mic 7:18,19; Zec 3:4 → feeds #14); **remembered / marked / counted** (Num 5:15; Hos 8:13; Psa 32:2; 130:3 → feeds #13); **confessed** (Lev 16:21; 26:40; Psa 38:18; 32:5). The borne-wrong (priest/Servant) vs borne-penalty (Eze 4:4–6) ambiguity rides on the G/I boundary.
- **⚑ SYNTH — the accumulation / measure register (AV §2e, feeds #18).** a.von is great / full / heavy / counted: "iniquity of the Amorites is not yet complete" (Gen 15:16); "iniquities have gone over my head; like a heavy burden" (Psa 38:4; cf. 40:12); "our iniquities have risen higher than our heads … mounted up to the heavens" (Ezr 9:6,7,13); "no end to your iniquities" (Job 22:5); "iniquity of Ephraim is bound up … kept in store" (Hos 13:12); "double iniquity" (Hos 10:10).
- **⚑ SYNTH — guilt is the liability the core incurs (R2g §2).** The guilt-band (a.sham/ash.mah/a.shem) touches the sin-core directly: cha.ta ×7, chat.tat ×5, a.von ×5, pe.sha ×1, ma'al ×3. Guilt is **not a separate wrong but the answerability that attaches to the core** — "if anyone sins … and realizes his guilt" (Lev 4–6); "he shall bear his iniquity" with guilt (Lev 5:17). The clearest extension/aspect relation in the family.
- **⚑ SYNTH — the conscience operation: realize-guilt → confess (R2g §3).** The recurring Levitical sequence "when he comes to know it and **realizes his guilt** … and **confesses** the sin" (Lev 4:13,22,27; 5:3–5; 6:4; Num 5:6) — a.sham is the verb of coming-to-awareness; the strongest inner-being *process* in the guilt-band (guilt as something the inner being comes to *know*). Further: **guilt borne / mounting as a weight** ("bear their guilt" with "their heart is false" Hos 10:2, lev co-seated; "guilt has mounted up to the heavens" Ezr 9:6); **guilt coupled with shame** ("I am ashamed and blush … our guilt mounted up" Ezr 9:6, bosh/kalam co-occur); **guilt drives the turn to God** ("until they acknowledge their guilt and seek my face … earnestly seek me" Hos 5:15). Also Isa 53:10 ("when his soul makes an offering for guilt") and the guilt-offering noun a.sham (1Sa 6; Pro 14:9; Ezr 10:19) = the **remedy** sense → cross-ref #14.
- **⚑ SYNTH — pu.qah = staggering of the conscience (R1 §2, §3).** pu.qah (H6330, 1 occ) reaches **heart + conscience** explicitly: "no … pang of **conscience**" (1Sa 25:31) — a genuine inner-being seat. The one Ring-1 dynamic that names the conscience faculty directly. **↔ BOND M03** (the conscience/inner-disquiet cluster). Note: pu.qah CORE-touches = 0 (it lives with the inner being, not the sin-core lexemes).
- **⚠ HYGIENE — the ne.phesh-as-person idiom (the key flag; AV §3, R2g §4, R1 §3).** Of a.von's 9 ne.phesh co-seatings, several read as person/life, NOT an interior seat — "you will have delivered your soul [yourself]" (Eze 3:19); "soul: myself" tags (Lev 7:18; 26:43); "anguish of his soul" = the Servant's life (Isa 53:11); "soul: appetite" (Eze 7:19; Hos 4:8); "soul: life" (1Sa 20:1; Jer 51:6). Likewise the guilt-band location=soul artefacts (Lev 4:27; 5:2,4,17; Num 5:6 = the "if anyone (nephesh) … realizes his guilt" legal idiom; Psa 34:22 nephesh="life"). Treat all as person/life, NOT soul-seating.
- **⚠ HYGIENE — genuine heart-seats only (cite lev/le.vav; AV §2f).** The interior is **bounded, not pervasive** — 7 genuine heart-seatings of 207 (a.von) + the guilt-band's Hos 10:2. **Do not over-read a.von as heart-seated.** Genuine **lev "heart" (5):** "Do not let the king take it to heart [hold guilty]" (2Sa 19:19); "take away the iniquity … David's heart struck him" (2Sa 24:10); "my iniquities have overtaken me … my heart fails me" (Psa 40:12); "her iniquity is pardoned … speak to her heart" (Isa 40:2); "the iniquity of his unjust gain … the way of his own heart" (Isa 57:17). **le.vav "heart" (2):** "if their uncircumcised heart is humbled … make amends for their iniquity" (Lev 26:41); "your iniquity … your heart said" (Jer 13:22). **she.er (1)** Lev 20:19 = kin-flesh, NOT interior. **ba.sar (1)** Hos 8:13 = sacrificial flesh, NOT interior.
- **⚠ HYGIENE — other field flags (AV §3, R2g §4, R1 §3).** Object text vs object_type: trust object_type (Gen 4:13 object="Lord" but object_type=God = what Cain bears, not the Lord). lemma_meaning is uniformly "crime" across ALL three sub-entries — the guilt/punishment sense distinctions live only in gloss/sense, **do not infer the tri-fold from lemma_meaning**. sense "iniquity" vs "iniquities" = number, not a sense split (cosmetic). The H5771I punishment sense is descriptive of a penalty yet tagged `sinful` — flag whether penalty-borne should read sinful or external-pole-neutral. Guilt-band: Psa 69:5 spurious origin=received-from-outside (no external source); Psa 5:10 Hiphil = causative ("make them bear their guilt," God holding guilty).
- **⚖ BORDER — #17 vs #18 split (guilt-state vs accumulated-crime).** Both units draw from the same a.von lemma; the split is by face — #18 takes the CRIME / act-classification + accumulation face (H5771G; faces a, e), #17 takes the GUILT / inner-liability face (H5771H + the a.sham guilt-band; face b). The PUNISHMENT face (H5771I) belongs to neither (external-pole; see SYNTH above). Per-occurrence verse→unit assignment is by reading, not by sub-entry alone; **deferred to §10** except where noted salient in the sub-sections.
- **↔ BOND — cross-cluster.** **M41 (Remembrance)** — the remembered/marked/counted register (a.von brought-to-remembrance, not-remembered); **M23** (Strength/Power/Dominion — the borne-burden weight); **M26** (Righteousness — guilt vs the clean/innocent); **M25** (Life — "the soul who bears iniquity"); **M47 (Constitution)** — the heart/conscience seats (lev/le.vav, and pu.qah's conscience); **M03** (pu.qah, the conscience-stagger). Also #13 (divine record), #14 (forgiveness/remedy), #15 (generational) via the borne/visited/blotted-out registers.

---

### Unit #18 — Iniquity as accumulated moral crime
- **DEF (DB):** the inner dimension of accumulated wrongdoing — crime in the moral-spiritual sense; iniquity as a measured, accruing, generational, heart-seated standing wrong. Not the act in isolation but the **moral crime that mounts up, is bound in store, and is counted/remembered**. The constitutive "iniquity" register of the inner life.
- **Term:** a.von **H5771G** (the dominant sub-entry, "iniquity: crime"; sense iniquity/iniquities + "crime"). Object_type for this face overwhelmingly abstract or none.
- **Salient (AV faces a, e):** the act-itself, unbounded/accruing — Gen 15:16 ("iniquity of the Amorites not yet complete"); Job 13:26 ("iniquities of my youth"); Psa 51:5 ("brought forth in iniquity"); Deu 19:15 ("any crime … any wrong," sense="crime"); Job 31:11,28. **Accumulation/measure:** Psa 38:4 ("gone over my head; like a heavy burden"); 40:12; Ezr 9:6,7,13 ("risen higher than our heads … to the heavens"); Job 22:5 ("no end to your iniquities"); Hos 13:12 ("bound up … kept in store"); Hos 10:10 ("double iniquity"); Psa 25:11 ("for it is great").
- **Signature:** type=status; faculty=none (term-intrinsic); valence sinful; the heart-seated/measured/generational register.
- **⚑ SYNTH:** the accumulation register (great/full/heavy/bound-up-in-store) is a **cross-verse process** (iniquity mounting over time/over a people), not visible per-occurrence — needs a verse-narrative pass to evidence the accrual. **Surface.**
- **↔ BOND:** #13 (divine record — counted/remembered iniquity), #15 (generational — "visiting the iniquity of the fathers"), M41 (Remembrance). M23 (the heavy borne burden).

### Unit #17 — Guilt as inner-being state
- **DEF (DB):** the conscience's recognition of moral liability before God — the subjective inner guilt that **cannot be hidden**; the being-answerable-for that attaches to the inner person; guilt that is realized, confessed, borne as weight, coupled with shame, and drives the turn to God.
- **Terms:** a.von **H5771H** (guilt) · a.von **H5771I** (punishment — *cross-flag: edges to external pole, see SYNTH*) · the guilt-liability band **a.sham (H0816)** · **a.shem (H0818)** · **ash.mah (H0819)** · the conscience-stagger **pu.qah (H6330)** (*cross-flag M03*).
- **Salient (AV face b; R2g §3):** the incurred answerable-for, forensic/self-protestation — Gen 44:16 ("God has found out the guilt of your servants"); 1Sa 20:1 ("What is my guilt? … my sin"); 1Sa 20:8; 2Sa 14:32; **"On me alone be the guilt"** (1Sa 25:24; 2Sa 14:9 — guilt taken upon the speaker); Job 11:6; Neh 4:5 ("Do not cover their guilt"); 2Sa 22:24 = Psa 18:23 ("I kept myself from guilt"). **The conscience operation:** realize-guilt → confess (Lev 4:13,22,27; 5:3–5; 6:4; Num 5:6). **Guilt as weight:** Hos 10:2 (borne, "their heart is false," lev); Ezr 9:6,7,13. **Guilt + shame:** Ezr 9:6 (bosh/kalam). **Guilt → seek God:** Hos 5:15. **pu.qah:** 1Sa 25:31 ("no pang of conscience").
- **Signature:** the inner-liability + conscience register; the genuine heart/conscience seats (lev Hos 10:2; conscience 1Sa 25:31) concentrate here.
- **⚖ BORDER:** H5771I (punishment) is listed under #17's terms for collation completeness, but its penalty-borne face is **external-pole, not inner-being** (see §A SYNTH) — verse→home for the punishment occurrences is deferred to §10.
- **↔ BOND:** **M03** (pu.qah — conscience/inner-disquiet); **M47 (Constitution)** (heart/conscience seats); M26 (Righteousness — guilt vs innocence); #14 (Forgiveness — the guilt-offering a.sham remedy sense, 1Sa 6; Pro 14:9; Ezr 10:19); #3 (Confession — realize→confess sequence).

---
